Reflection on Heart Realm
The title of today's message is 'Reflection on Heart Realm.' Here, the '체' (体) in 체휼 refers to the body, and the '휼' (恤) means heart. (While writing) This (心) is the heart, and this (血) is blood. Therefore, 체휼 signifies the experience of the heart. It is quite different from the English word 'experience.' Ultimately, the experience of the heart leads to love.

Everyone, a person cannot feel tears, sadness, or pain through mere experience. The experience of the heart encompasses such content. It connects immediately with tears, sadness, pain, and joy. Therefore, the life of reflection is directly linked to tears, sadness, and all forms of suffering.

Everyone, wouldn't it be wonderful if this word could unite us? (Laughter) You feel it, right? The barrier of words is immense. Through words, all external and internal worlds are connected.

Now, when we look at God as the center, where does the origin of human speech lie? If we trace it back through our ancestors, we eventually reach God, the absolute being, and the relationship between God and humanity. Then, why do we need words? It is to benefit everything about ourselves. When we consider words, where should we place their purpose? There must be a center. So, what is the most beloved word? Think about it.

Today, those who are learning to gain knowledge, those majoring in literature, talk about Shakespeare, and scientists praise various famous figures in their fields, but words diverge into such content. However, what becomes the mainstream word among them? Ultimately, it is a matter of the heart. The central purpose is whether the heart can express joy.

Here, the term 체휼 refers to the heart's blood. What can excite and stir the heart? What could it be? Beauty? "No." Ultimately, the conclusion is love. Everything must be tied to the word love. All humanity, whether past, present, or future, transcending the borders of the world, when asked what cannot be complained about, the answer is nothing but love. Do you think so? "Yes."

When a person follows the heart, they can connect anywhere.
Now, looking at this, a person’s words and actions must be in harmony. This is called harmony of words and actions. In the East, this harmony is emphasized. What does that mean? It means that one must act according to what their heart can excite. Then, what is action? As mentioned earlier, if words express the heart and show love, then action is behavior centered around love. Therefore, the conclusion that these must align is quite fitting.

Then, what does 'I' like? What should I like? Ultimately, one should love to act according to love. Such a person will represent history, the present, the future, and even the spiritual world. The spiritual world connects with the human world. It is a principle. Everything can be concluded from this.

So, why do I see? Why do I hear? What do my senses aim to follow? We must understand all of this. Everything moves according to actions, so we can conclude that we want to be governed by actions aimed at love and wish to comply with love.

Then, what kind of person is a pitiful person, and what kind of person is a happy person? This is the question. What kind of person is happy? Can we say, "A person with a lot of money who doesn't work and just plays is a happy person"? That cannot be true. Some may think they are happy because they know a lot and have much knowledge, saying, "Ah, I know more than anyone else." But such a person is not happy either. Also, there may be someone who becomes a president of a country and thinks they will be happy with power, but that is also a wrong thought.

So, what do you see as happiness? Where is the starting point of happiness? "Love." Ultimately, it is love. Love, love. (Laughter) This is the same for people of the past, present, and future; it is all unified.

If God created us to face such humanity, what kind of God would that be? It is the same. If you ask God, "Are you happy?" He would answer, "Yes, but when I cannot find love, I am unhappy. I cannot stand in the place of true happiness." This is an undeniable conclusion. It naturally becomes so. One cannot avoid this conclusion. From this perspective, even if God is omniscient and omnipotent, He cannot enjoy true happiness by Himself. Then, who is needed to complete that happiness? 'I' am needed. I am necessary.

Now, what is the problem here? God is eternal. (While writing) God does not need air or moisture like humans do. Even with His eyes open, He must be thought of as eternally awake. Does God have a nose? (Laughter) Does He need air like you do? The nose is for breathing air. (Laughter) When you think that way, it is unnecessary. If there is no air in heaven, does God need ears? You must understand that such questions are fundamental issues.

If we say God does not need the five senses, would you prefer a vague God? (Laughter) If so, there are no relative conditions to praise God using literary terms like "lovely eyes like a dove" or "lips like..." (Laughter) 

Do you like such a God? Would you prefer such a God? (Laughter) When you think that way, ultimately, we cannot help but establish the concept that we need a God who is like us, or even more handsome than us. We need a God who is greater than us, a God who is perfect in every way. (Laughter) Just because something is great does not mean it is great in the way we consume it. The 'greatness' is of a different nature. Ultimately, what does greatness mean? It means being more beautiful, more lovable, and better than me. That is what it means. Everything is different.

The realm of heart is the realm where God's love connects.
Now, what is being discussed today is the heart realm. What is the scope of the heart realm? What exactly is the heart realm? The heart realm encompasses all of creation. Therefore, what is the heart? The heart refers to the affection of the heart. Wherever there is affection of the heart, it belongs to the heart realm. Why is that? Because God created it, the flow of God's heart is already internally connected there. Therefore, we can make this deduction. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Electricity, you see, uses external power... What is it? If you look at an electric wire and say, "Hey, electricity, go this way," does the light turn on? Even if the earth has the power to collide and break apart, if you say, "Hey, turn on the light," does it turn on? "No." Why doesn't it turn on? Electricity must flow. Only then does the light turn on. Now, with God's heart realm, if only God's heart flows, the universe operates that way. Other things may not connect, but if only God's heart occupies it, it sticks together. (Hits someone in front playfully. Laughter) It’s okay to get hit once to wake someone up. (Laughter) Do you understand? What is the heart realm? It is the realm where God's love connects. If you think of it that way, it becomes very simple to understand. (Laughter. Applause) Do you understand the heart realm? "Yes."

What is the heart? The heart, the heart, the heart. But what is the realm of the heart? It is the realm where God's love connects. Then, "Ah," you should understand. Do you understand now? "Yes." If you don't understand, try grabbing electricity once. (Laughter) Then even those who were dozing off will suddenly (gestures) have their bodies activated. Those who were lying down will immediately rise. (Laughter) Do you understand now? "Yes."

Do you know what the heart realm is? You all do not know what the heart realm is right now. "What is the heart realm? What is the reflection on the heart realm that the teacher spoke about?" You might think that way. It is the realm where God's love connects. What is reflection? It is feeling that electricity, saying "Oh!" That is reflection. It is feeling how strong it is. It is feeling whether it is good or not.

Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." You must firmly grasp the concept of reflection. This is quite extensive.

As mentioned earlier, the heart realm has the content that can connect everything. There is nothing that does not belong to this heart realm; anywhere, the electric connection of the heart can occur. Electricity is quite interesting; when there is a complete negative, a positive automatically arises. Likewise, when there is a complete positive, a negative automatically arises. It has that harmony. Why is that? It is because of the cause.

Now, what is the electric connection of the heart? It is the electric connection of love, akin to positive electricity. When we look at people, it is like negative electricity centered around love. It is the electric connection of love. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Electricity is the same, right? (Points to what he wrote) The earth conducts electricity well. What does electricity seek? The earth. When it meets the earth, it just flows.

So, what about God? God is the subject of love like electricity, and that subject wants to work through people. Do you understand what I mean? Everything is related in that way. That is why it is said that antennas must be high. Why do we erect antennas? Because there is electricity in the air, positive electricity. The higher it is, the closer it gets to that. Therefore, on the ground, it is said that antennas must be high. Do you understand? "Yes."

The heart can connect directly to heaven.
This is the same for humans, so humans also say, "Raise the antenna, raise the antenna, raise it, raise it." You may not see it, but there are antennas coming out from the top of your heads. They may be thick, tall, thin, or in countless states. That is a fact. (Laughter)

So, what is love? It is like this receiving device. If the antenna is high and the receiver is good, everything comes in. 

What is that? Through the frequency of love, through the antenna, I feel the touch of love resonating within me like radar. When I think of that, does it feel good or bad? "Good." How much? "Very much." So, it fills the universe. The concept that it can fill the universe arises. Since electricity flows, it goes "beep beep..." (Laughter)

Then it becomes a power plant. It becomes a broadcasting station. Therefore, the heart realm connects everywhere; this is theoretical.

Because He created it, He has the subjective ability to analyze emotions through the frequency of love, which makes it possible.

Similarly, when we look at 'me,' I also have such abilities. (Laughter) Do you understand? If I am happy, the universe is happy, and if I smile, the whole universe smiles. We must understand this concept. Now, if God exists, would you go to Him or not? Would you move God or not? "I would." If that is true, how wonderful would that be?

Therefore, we must understand that what we need is the heart; we need the heart. Here, the heart refers to the mind. It is the center of the heart. Do you understand? The heart can connect directly to heaven.

That's love. That's what love is. If I am present, I should do more than when I am absent. Why do you go around looking for people? "To love myself." When you oppose and fight back, the bundle of love in your heart bursts. It leaves you. So you must endure. Our Identity  
When we talk about "identity," you will naturally think about whether that concept is good or bad.  
The Unification Church judges the right and wrong of identity based on heart and love.  
When we talk about "the identity of America" or "the identity of the American people," there naturally arises the concept of good Americans and bad Americans when viewing the country of America and the American people. Also, if there is an ideal world, when viewing the world through that ideal worldview, some countries are seen as good countries, and some as bad countries; you naturally think like that.  
So, while that is true on a large scale, if we look at individuals, individuals also have that position, and families, tribes, nations, and the entire world are all in that position. The spirit world is the same.  
So what can be the center? What is the standard that distinguishes good from bad? In terms of America, America judges right and wrong based on its past, present, and future history. That is undeniable. It is bound to be judged based on history. What comes next? In that era, laws are centered around judgment. Today, in America, there are current laws.  
68  
So how do laws work? They are made to fit the times. Therefore, sometimes they may go against tradition. What comes next? Our moral and ethical lives become the standard for all criticism. Generally, that’s how it is viewed. When you look at it this way, history, current laws, and ethics generally become the criteria for judging the right and wrong of identity.  
While that is generally the case, when viewed from a religious perspective, there is one more level. In our Unification Church, we are centered not on ethics but on heart. We are centered on love. From that perspective, when we say "we," we think of "our Unification Church." Then when we say "I," we think of "I, a member of the Unification Church." So today, I want to talk about "our identity."  
Then how is the history of the Unification Church? History is the issue. Who makes history? You all think simply. You must think that the history of the Unification Church has complex content. When we ask who made the history of the Unification Church, we can say, "Reverend Moon made it," or "we made it," and further, from God's perspective, we can say, "God made it." They are all the same.  
Now, all of that is correct, but it cannot be just God’s side, nor just Reverend Moon, nor just you. It cannot be separate. When God thinks of the restoration history of the Unification Church, He cannot say, "I made it." Before thinking of Himself as God, He must think that there is Reverend Moon and there are members of the Unification Church. When you think of that, when you say, "Oh, we made it," the concept of "Oh, God made it and the teacher made it" must first be established among "us."  
So, who comes first, I or the teacher, or God? Who comes first? What is the order? It’s all mixed up; what is the order? What is the order? There must be order. When you think of that, God comes first. Then comes the teacher. Then comes you. Now, can you see God? God is invisible. Because He is invisible, we have no choice but to align ourselves with the teacher, who is visible, in a central position. This conclusion arises.  
When you focus on the central figure, the whole becomes yours.  
When these three go, if God raises His right foot, should the teacher raise his left foot? What about you? Should you raise your left foot? God has a big stride.
If we go like this, can the teacher take two steps, two steps (expressing with gestures)? If the walking stride is big, it means you just have to go slowly. You have to match it while saying one, two, one, two.

Do you walk like this? You can't walk like this. You can't make even one mistake. So when you say, "Walk to the left," is it enough to just say "Oh"? (expressing with gestures) When you say "Go to the right," you have to go to the right, and when you say "Go to the left," you have to go like this. Is that correct or not? Yes, no? "Yes." No! "Yes." No! "Yes." No! "Yes!" (laughter)

Then why do we have to do that? Why do we have to match with the center person? It's to become one. When we become one, what happens? When we become one, the whole becomes mine. Our things become my things. Our things become my things. The whole becomes mine. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Why do we have to become one? Why? The reason we have to follow is that the whole becomes our things, my things. What that means is, the members of the Unification Church who match their steps, all the things of the Unification Church become the possessions of those individuals. It's the same.

Now, from a historical perspective, why did it turn out this way? When we become one with history, everything that appears in that historical process becomes mine. Do you understand? The Jews have tradition, but why do they have that? It's because everything that has been achieved in Judaism historically becomes mine. Do you understand what I mean? Does it seem like that? There is that meaning.

From the historical perspective I mentioned earlier, then from the perspective of contemporary life, from the ethical perspective, and from the emotional perspective, it becomes the same. The principle is the same. Think about it, is it so or not? If we align everything around American law, then everything under American law becomes mine. In other words, it becomes my country at the same time. That's how it works. Do you understand? "Yes."

The same goes for ethical issues. Even if there is strict morality centered around ethics, by adhering to it, it becomes our ethical world but also my world.

What is the heart that the Unification Church talks about today? What does it mean when we say it's God's heart, emotional? When we do fundraising, evangelizing, and sacrificing, even if I don't want to, I have to do it. What about you? When I say, "Lift your right foot," do you lift your left foot? "No." What is it? Let's think about our identity from this perspective. When we think about the past, did I pass? How many years has it been since I joined the Unification Church? To go to Florida from here, you need to wear summer clothes. Everyone here is wearing winter clothes. When someone who doesn't know sees this, they might say, "Huh? Why are you taking winter clothes? Why not take summer clothes?" If you don't want to take summer clothes, you can just wear them. When your parents see you changing into summer clothes, they might say, "Hey, you crazy kid! What's wrong with you? It's so cold, why are you wearing summer clothes?" The person preparing to go to Florida wins. Who is more foolish? Who is the more foolish person?

The Standard of Good and Bad 
I sincerely thank all of you, the heads of the city, county, and district branches who have gathered from all over the country to attend this event. Through such gatherings, we must seek ways for this country to develop and for our homeland to contribute to the history of humanity, and we must pioneer the path where that can be sought. I have always thought that this is the responsibility of the people of our homeland whom Heaven has protected. 

First of all, I thank you for gathering like this after a long time. Everyone, let’s have a free atmosphere. I hope you can think like students at this time, and since I am standing on this platform, I hope you can recognize me as a teacher, and I wish for us to have a free atmosphere where we can ask and answer each other. 

On this day, the title or content of what I want to say to you may be "Good and Bad," "Good and Evil." I would like to share a few words on this topic. 

Whenever we face any matter in our daily lives, the issue we confront is whether this matter ends as a good thing or a bad thing. It is inevitably decided as one of these two. From small matters to large ones, whether centered around the family, through society, through the nation, or regardless of any existence in the world, in the process they face, it is an undeniable fact that they will inevitably bring about a result that is either good or bad. There are good and bad things in what we hear, good and bad things in what we see, good and bad things in what we say, and good and bad things in what we do; this is true throughout our daily lives. 

From this perspective, what is it that we humans like the most? This is the most important question when considering the history of humanity. What is the most precious thing, and what is the best thing? When we ponder this, some may say that money is the best, some may say that power is the best, and some may say that knowledge is the best, but is that truly what humanity desires the most? It is not just that. 

So, what is the best thing? Some people wish for the best centered on themselves. The majority of people think this way. They may wish for their family to be the best, and furthermore, they may wish for their country to be the best, and for the world they live in to be the best. This is the thought that arises. 

Then, what is the best among these? This is ultimately not something centered on oneself but a relative concept. It cannot escape relative relationships. When viewed this way, what is the best in a family? To conclude, is it not that parents are the best? Money is good, knowledge is good, and power is good, but for me, the best and most precious thing is parents. Then, what is next? It is the beloved wife or husband. And when asked what comes next, we can only conclude that it is the beloved children. 

God also needs a counterpart to experience love. 

So why are parents good, and why are husbands and wives good, and why are children good? It is because love is involved. The love of parents is an absolutely necessary love for children. True love between husband and wife is an absolutely necessary love for them. Brotherly love or the filial piety of children towards parents is the most precious thing. 

Then, when we look at the world centered on humanity, will it be woven only with love centered on the family? To elevate the dimension, for example, if God exists, what would be the thing that God loves the most? This is a serious question. What does God love? 

Since God is omniscient and omnipotent, He does not need knowledge, power, or money. So what is it that God needs? It is a being that God can love. What must that being be? It must be no one other than the most precious and the highest being among all creation. Then, if we say that the most lovable being for God is humanity, why does God love that person? It is because God also needs love. Love cannot be known alone. 

As you all know, when we think of the period of youth, or before adolescents enter puberty, they cannot feel whether they have love or not. When the puberty stage arrives and a counterpart appears, they finally come to feel that they have love. 

God is the same. In order for God to experience love, a counterpart is also needed. We can understand here that love is not something that comes from oneself but is found through a counterpart. 

So, what did God and humanity establish as the center of their relationship? It is love. It is through love that we have goodness, happiness, and everything finds its place. 

Today, this love is not the mundane love of our human world. The omniscient and absolute love of God must be absolute once it is given. Therefore, the true person who can stand before such love, the true person is the issue.

Therefore, even if I have to bend my back, I must visit every village. Even if my shoes wear out, even if my clothes tear, I must go." (Applause) You must do that. Perhaps the largest province is Gyeongsangbuk-do. The head of the Gyeongsangbuk-do chapter is in a tough spot. (Laughter) If he thinks, "Oh, this person is saying good things, but when I think about it, it's a big deal," then he can give up his position as the head of the chapter. (Laughter)

Without this method, we cannot save the country. No matter how much money someone has, can they earn enough to feed the Republic of Korea? No, they cannot. We must share the responsibility. Look, if I have become the root, then my root has no rest. A single branch has no rest. In the eight provinces, the branches of the eight provinces have no rest. The districts are branches. Each province has 20 branches. Those 20 branches have no rest. And among those 20 branches, there are numerous villages. How many villages? Is it 1,669 villages? Those villages have no rest. And even the small branches of 60,000 ri have no rest. Everyone is responsible. Who can play around? Each branch must work tirelessly to sprout.

So, where do flowers bloom? Flowers do not bloom from the trunk. Do flowers bloom from the branches of the tree or from the leaves? "They bloom from the branches." What? You answered incorrectly. (Laughter) They bloom from where the leaves grow, from where the leaves grow. So, what are the leaves of the Republic of Korea? They are families. The heads of households centered around the unit of the village. You must understand that.

I told the chairman of the Victory and Unity Federation, "Hey, this is the most critical time for the Republic of Korea, and if we cannot determine the direction in this chaotic period, we must become a lighthouse to show the way." You all know that we held a national security unification conference, right? National security unification conference! Because we held this conference, some people said, "Oh, this person is trying to become president." It is not about the president of the Republic of Korea. (Laughter) The world is the issue, the world. The problem is how to stop communism.

Look, how do we stop China and the Soviet Union? I am trying to carry out the core actions that can stop them. Because I was born as a citizen of the Republic of Korea, I want to do it through the people of the Republic of Korea. That is my thought. If I were Japanese, I would want to do it through the Japanese people. Why? Because I know that through this, I can receive blessings from the world.

The reason we must organize down to the village level. 

Whether anyone acknowledges it or not, just as life begins to sprout when winter passes and the ice begins to melt, we must not miss the timing and do what we must do. The issue is organization. How far must we organize? We must organize down to the village level. Then how should education be conducted? It is not about the governor, the county head, or the village chief; the issue is the housewives. We must center around the heads of households and the mothers and fathers of families and set the direction for everything.

Where do flowers bloom? They do not bloom from the province. Do you understand? "Yes." Do not boast about being the head of the provincial chapter. The head of the provincial chapter cannot bloom flowers. No matter how hard they try, they cannot bloom flowers. There is nothing to be upset about. (Laughter) Also, the head of the county chapter cannot bloom flowers, no matter how loudly they speak. Do you understand? The head of the village chapter is the same. Today, even though the heads of the village chapters are gathered, they might think, "Oh, I must be the head of the village chapter," but you cannot do it either. The head of the village chapter cannot bloom flowers. Who blooms flowers? It is the heads of the village chapters. (Laughter, applause)

So, knowing this, this person, who is aware, even if they have no money and are in debt, organizes down to the village level. They organize down to the village level and are more enthusiastic than the heads of the provincial chapter, county chapter, or village chapter. They are told to be enthusiastic, to be enthusiastic, to be fervent like the roots of love. Then flowers will bloom. What flowers? "The flowers of love." The flowers of love will bloom. (Laughter)

Then whether it is the Unification Church or the Victory and Unity Federation, it does not matter! When the day comes for flowers to bloom, we will be intoxicated by their fragrance and fall over. (Laughter, applause) Then we will say, "Oh, I would be happy even if I die! Oh, oh!" You know bees well. I know them well because we used to keep many bees at home. Bees that have gone through winter know the taste of honey very well. When they taste real honey, they do not know whether they will live or die. (Laughter)

There is something called consumption. It is the house of the bees. When spring comes, they clear out everything they ate during winter. They go out to the spring garden and gather honey. The bees that eat that honey, even if you pull their back end with tweezers, they will hold on with their four legs and will not let go, even if their back breaks. Try it. (Laughter) The taste is so good that they do not even realize their waist is gone. (Laughter)

So, if flowers bloom that are even better than that honey, what do you think will happen? When that happens, God… Who is the first to smell the fragrance? It is not the hunting dogs of the neighborhood. It is not the old men of the neighborhood. The old men do not sleep and guard the house 24 hours, so it is not them. It is not the children either. Who is the first to smell that fragrance? It is God who smells it first. Do you understand?

When God smells the fragrance, what happens? God comes to visit. "Hey, God is coming to our neighborhood, to this thatched house." Think about it. When God comes and tastes the sweetness, He becomes delighted. (Laughter)

And when you are embraced in His arms, once you are held, He does not let go. He does not let go. So what will happen? Will God bite and tear you away? Therefore, He has no choice but to say, "Ah, I cannot give you everything I have," and He blesses you for eternity. This is not just talk.

Today, I will give you a homework assignment… You might think, "Who is this President Moon?" but whether you like it or not, you must do it. And now, I hope that if someone does not voluntarily go, they will be pushed out even if someone has to hit them. That is my wish. So what do I want? I want you to become a branch that can bloom flowers in the village. Therefore, if you can create branches that can bloom flowers in the Republic of Korea first, that tree, which could have become a tree without branches, will be granted the qualification to survive because of the flowers blooming in that village and that village. For whom? For God.

Based on what of God? Based on God's love. You must understand this amazing fact. Do you want to do that? "Yes." Do you really want to do it? "Yes." Since I am meeting you for the first time, I cannot trust all of you. (Laughter) Even those who have believed for decades have run away, so how can I trust those I see for the first time? "Try believing once." Then, if you feel good about it, let those who want to do it raise their hands. "Wow." (Applause)

I believe there will be blessings in your families… Today, I hurriedly talked and jumped around a bit.

Every household must diligently bloom the flower of love.

Now, if you understand this… With the heart of a parent, the head of the provincial chapter must care for the county, the head of the county must care for the village, and the head of the village must care for the village unit. The heads of the village chapters must care for each household. "May flowers bloom in this house. May flowers bloom in our province." If you sincerely care for the province, the county, and the village unit, the Republic of Korea will become the center of fragrance in the world.

I asked this chairman to organize this, and I am grateful for the organization you have formed. Centered around the 63,000 ri of the Republic of Korea—if we take 40 million people and assume four people per household, how many is that? It is 10 million households—if love's flowers can bloom in 10 million households, God will absolutely not let the Republic of Korea perish. Anyone who comes to destroy will be struck by lightning. If they come believing in their strong legs, their legs will break. If they come believing in their strong eyes, their eyes will be knocked out. If they come believing in their strong hands, their hands will be twisted… You must know that it is impossible to perish if you know this. (Applause)

Knowing this, you must now hold onto one household… God is the same. God has worked hard holding onto one individual, saying that it is the path for the world, while holding onto one family. Thus, even someone like me, who has worked for thousands of years, God has thought, "Ah, there is value in holding onto individuals."

More than my individual self, families like that must emerge in the Republic of Korea, and through those families, numerous tribes must arise, and through those tribes, nations must form. When we stand before the world, the entire world will long for God's love, and we will automatically be able to connect with God's love as a central nation. When viewed this way, this is the path of patriotism above all else.

All the leaders of this country must also do the same. From the president down to everyone in office, they must sincerely care for the households at the grassroots level. Do not disregard this. You must not disregard it. Just because I have become something does not mean I can do everything as I please. It cannot be done that way. The heavenly law does not allow it. Who wants to perish? Who does not want to prosper? When one does not comply with the principles and laws, they are bound to perish, and when they comply with the principles and laws, they are bound to prosper. Know that the universe will help with that. I sincerely hope that you…
Today is the first day we met, but I don't know when we will meet again. I am busy. I have a busy way back.  
323  
Each branch leader should have a sincere heart for each household. With such thoughts, I have traveled through South Korea to Japan... Now, there are quite a few people in Japan who respect me. The same goes for America and South America.  
Now that we have entered a stage where we can move the nation, I cannot stay in South Korea for long. Therefore, I hope that you will expand South Korea here and take on such a mission, and I wish for you to become sons and daughters of heaven in God's love. May you become a family where the man is a prince of heaven and the woman is a princess of heaven, living with God forever, for a thousand years and ten thousand years!  
We have a good song in Korea, right? "Oh moon, bright moon! / The moon that played in Taebaek! / In that moon over there / The cassia tree is stuck / With a golden axe, cut it out / With a silver axe, trim it / Bringing my parents here / Living for a thousand years and ten thousand years / Bringing my parents here / Living for a thousand years and ten thousand years." Isn't there such a song?  
It is about bringing our parents here and living for a thousand years and ten thousand years. What does "parents" mean? Isn't it our country's dream to bring our heavenly parents into our home and live for a thousand years and ten thousand years? Isn't this the dream of our nation?  
Knowing that, you branch leaders should not stop your tearful steps for each household and village, and the county branch leaders should not complain saying, "Oh, the provincial branch leader is diligent, that young provincial branch leader is working hard." Instead, they should say, "Oh, what a wonderful provincial branch leader!" and respect each other while working for each household. The township branch leaders and the village branch leaders should do the same. When you all can manifest God's love from a position of serving, that country will surely be called heaven.  
Think about it. There is no other way to create one world than this method. Think about it. It cannot be done with political means, nor with economic means. I hope you all understand this and have made a promise... I am a man who believes well, so I trust you, and I wish for blessings to be upon your families and your provincial, county, and township branches. I ask you to become heavenly sons and daughters who can receive God's love, and I will conclude my remarks. Thank you. (Applause) *
